# FILECLONING #
# Script run termux
```  
pkg update
pkg upgrade
pkg install git
pkg install python
pkg install python2 
pip2 install requests
pip2 install mechanize
pip install lolcat
rm -rf FILECLONING
git clone https://github.com/MRVIVEK-CODER/FILECLONING.git
 cd FILECLONING
python2 Vivek67.max
```
